國外要電

西班牙帝制不絕如縷 32

王室濫用特權民怨沸騰

共和勢力激張大勢已去

西王電召自由黨魁組閣

路透社十五日瑪德里電　西班牙全國人心極端激張、首都及各工業大城尤甚、此間示威運動終日不絕、且明白要求國王遜位及取銷帝制、已不復視修改憲法爲满意、祗望國王速死之呼聲時時可聞、某次且有大隊民衆圖攻監獄、釋放日前革命案中被拘諸人、但卒爲警察與保安隊所驅散、京外如撒拉古薩·巴塞洛那·伐倫西亞·格拉拿達塞維拉·及其他大市鎭、情形如出一轍、總之共和勢力業已　漫各處、目下主要問題、祇爲軍隊何時加入革命而已、但大多數人民均信此亦旦夕間事、

路透社十五日瑪德里電　康波今日抵此、覲見國王後、在陸軍部與貝倫格將軍會商一切、康波後發表一文、謂渠勸國王接受左派所組織之政府、國王現電致避居巴黎之自由黨領袖艾爾巴、促其立即返京、大約王將請艾爾巴組閣、一般輿情頗主張完全修改憲法、削減國王權力、就現象觀之、王現願服從極端左派、貝倫格語人、否認渠將往國外休養之說、渠欲稍留、以覓陸軍中相當位置、

路透社十五日巴黎電　西班牙自由黨領袖艾爾巴今夜於新聞記者詢以國王電促返國事時、不允作切實言論、但謂渠須俟國王依允修改西班牙君主之相沿政策時、始可返瑪里云、艾氏昨已接到國王請其立即返國之電、衆料王將囑渠組閣、按艾氏前由西班牙避居巴黎、爲政治逋客、

路透社十五日瑪德里電　喀　隆領袖康波致書某報、謂國家所需要者、旣非狄克推多詞、亦非革命、更非目前政　之維持、但僅欲受眞正德　克拉西之統治耳、　　路透社十五日瑪德里電　昨日此間各處發生小騒擾、共和黨不聽官塲禁令、在多處集會、警察屢驅散之、國王今日接見政治領袖多人、各向王陳述其對於將來政府之意見、

時評

西班牙政局之新趨勢 34

此次西班牙内閣之辭職。非内閣本身問題。而爲帝制存廢問題也爲内閣本。

身問題而辭職。苟後繼者選任得人。政局即可安定。爲帝制問題而牽動内閣。則非於君主與民主兩途。得一切實之解决。内閣改組而政局終不安定。西班牙人想望共和已久。一致主張非請西王遜位不可。而西王尙欲維持自身地位。急急於物色繼任之人。但稍明此中情勢者。不敢就此過渡之重任。故以吾人測之。今後情勢。不出兩途。一爲修改憲法削減國王權力。一爲重訂新憲法。實行民主政體。第一說爲一般溫和派所倡導。第二說則爲急進派與多數國民主張之。此後西王勢不得不從第一說。允許修改憲法。如今日自由黨領袖艾爾巴所言。須俟西王依允修改西班牙君主相之權力時。始可應西王之請而返國故能由此進行。艾氏返國組閣或亦可緩和一時者也。然此緩和一時之政策。終不能挽回主張澈底改革之人心。試觀喀泰隆領袖康波之言。謂今日西班牙所需要者。非狄克推多制。亦非無目的之革命更非目前政體之維持但祗欲得眞正德謨克拉西之統治耳。此言足以代表一般班西牙之人心。故僅修改憲法。減削王權决不能满西人之意。故非完全達到民主政治目的實行第二說則西班牙之共和運動。終不能一日停息。政局亦必不能一日安定此蓋可惟預斷者也。

中央與國府紀念週 40

中央黨部　二月十六日上午九時、中央黨部在大禮堂舉行第九十九次總理紀念週、到中央委員胡漢民·褚民誼·馬超俊·陳　英·王柏齡·余井塘、各部處會職員及來賓約五百餘人、胡漢民主席、行禮後、主席報告、略謂「自四中全會决定關於黨務之推進·黨員之工作·黨統之整飭·三種訓練方案、綱舉目張、繩意糾廖、乃爲一般同志所應奉作左右　銘、而服膺勿失者、須知爲黨服務、最要在一致動作、有進無退、以主義原則上所要求爲立足點、共同努力於整個政治上所要求、而副整個民衆之希望、現時黨務工作、所以有糾正必要之原因、乃心理上有一種錯誤、以爲軍閥已經剷除、大局漸臻統一、本黨工作、可以稍事雍容、不必十分緊張、更以達到安定爲已足、認爲動不如靜、故奮鬥進取之精神、因日漸减少、不知在破壞時期、旣以革命精神掃除一切障碍、現値建設時期、其責任比較爲尤要、而障碍亦甚多、乃工作反趨於消極、究將何以自解、琴瑟不調、改絃而更張之可也、若因不調、即棄絃而弗彈、乃等於因噎廢食、是烏乎可、本黨愉主義相結合、爲政治之機軸、若失其行動能力、則任何事業、必因而落後、尙何有於進取、更何有於建設、共產黨時用陰險手段、以分化本黨爲目的、如能整個團結、主義之工作、更日形緊張、則其計自無由得逞、共禍之消滅、亦非難事、本黨七命精神、在於知仁勇、而知與仁之致用、在賴勇以濟之、凡事肯於犧牲、即是大勇、就已往歷史觀察、無論軍事政治黨務、如負責之人、能具犧牲决心、斷舞不成功之理、現在反動派及帝國主義者之野心、尙未完全抛棄、黨之動作、固未可一步放鬆、即至反動派消滅帝國主義拱手退讓之時、亦必有適應需要之動作、以備不虞、未可泄泄沓沓、自誤事功、訓練之道、雖非是一端、其大要則在於動作不息、肯自犧牲、凡關於民衆方面、爲本黨義所當爲之事、隨時動員、不稍退縮、更須以合羣精神、一致動作、集羣策羣力、爲整個之大動員、訓練二字、本屬聯貫關繫、如治軍然、若訓而不練、則男氣必减、工作效率、難望增進云云、報告畢、十時散會、

日方則稱一人未傷

瀋陽通信、遼寗國民外交協會、頃得撫順满鐵煤礦大山本坑十八路·於八日午前十一時五十分突然發火、日方即將坑門封閉、傳有華工三千人喪命消息、當即派常識促進會總幹事車向辰·及會員郝克勇·李正文、即日前往調查、以明眞相、車氏於十一日始歸、據談抵撫後、先至敎育局及圖書館詢問、未得端倪、又化妝至炭坑附近調查、與礦工談話、藉以探訪、亦未得其詳、且受日警及守衛之干涉與阻止、最後始晤熟悉日方情形之報界某君詢問此事、據言礦坑確發炎、原因由於礦夫誤舉礦石上之硫磺、死傷華工約二三千人、惟據日方事後宣傳、謂該日爲星期、礦夫休息、故未傷人、但有下列疑點、（一）礦坑内雖星期、亦有工人在内、日方宣傳並未傷人、未免矯枉過正、（二）當發火時、礦工家屬多往坑側探望、報載死者達三千人、而事後日方宣傳竟一名未傷、矛盾過甚、車氏並謂此次失事、由於設備不良、我方應設法調查死傷確實人數、俾與日方據理交涉、令其賠償損失云云、

葉翼熊解瀋後地方法院公開審理 45

葉認妬婚而不認圖財

高法院裁判移瀋理由

瀋陽通信、前特區地方法院　易推　葉翼熊謀殺張麗卿案、業經　寗司法當局奉張司令令、將葉解瀋詢辦、葉已於八日解瀋、惟張麗卿因傷勢未愈、仍留哈醫治、尙未到瀋、葉解瀋後、地方法院一面將葉寄押们看守所、一面經檢查官薛　屏幾度偵查、已於十日提起公訴、十一日上午十時、地方法院特在刑庭開審、由庭長唐蔭芬承錄、檢查官薛　屏、亦同時出庭、十時二十分將葉由看守所提出、葉穿靑呢大鼈、戴土耳其皮、帽足帶　　、形容憔竹、首由法官略加審訊、檢查官即起立陳述起訴　、謂葉翼熊謀殺張麗卿經特區法院檢查處按侵佔殺人提起公訴、不爲不合、　　原起訴書提起公訴、請貴院依法公判、　由法官審訊葉殺人情形、葉直供認不諱、　僅供因妬婚行兇、不承認圖財害命、最後法官起立、宣告本案候原告到庭、定期再審、　即退庭、　仍由法警送押看守所

刑庭裁定葉翼熊預謀殺人未遂、及侵佔一案、最高法院東北分院刑事庭、根據最高法院東北分院檢查官聲請　解遼寗瀋陽地方法院　　第一　、其裁定理由如下、聲請人聲請意旨、稱查被告葉翼熊、前充東省特别區域地方法院候補推事、因預謀殺人未遂及侵佔案、由濱江地方法院書理、茲奉東北政務委員會電開、葉翼熊案、濱江法院推事執行職務、恐有不平之虞、應由該署聲請最高法院東北分院裁定、以瀋陽地方法院爲第一　法院、仰查照辦理具報等因奉此、查此案葉翼熊原來服務之法院、與濱江地方法院、在同一地域、雖濱江地方法院人員、未必盡與該被告相　、而審判上終恐有所偏倚、自應依刑事訴訟法第二十一條第二十二條聲請移轉遼寗瀋陽地方法院管轄、俾昭司法威信等語、本院按法院因特别情形、恐審判有不公平之虞者、在上級法院得將該案件移轉於其管轄内、與原法院同級之他法院、此在刑事訴訟法第二十一條有明文規定、本件被告人預謀殺人及侵佔一案、業已紫屬於濱江地方法院爲第一　審判、查該被告人、原係東省特别區域地方法院候補推事、與濱江地方法院係在同一地域、難保審判上無不公平之虞、聲請人聲請、應認爲有理由、應依刑事訴訟法第二十三條裁定、本案應移轉遼寗瀋陽地方示院管轄第一審、

金融結束日之金潮 74

發現空前紀錄

逼近八百兩關

飛跳起拾四兩四　昨二月十六日標金在此大結束期内、連生新紀錄、已衝出七百九十兩大關漲風加厲、循序甚佳惟盤頭不過二三兩至外滙以鬆爲緊、掛牌放長半　不　明寬暗　蓋洋商有結欵、各號心理趨堅市塲内求過於供、若永豐福昌源盛等皆有買進、元茂永元興永及　戶等大致脫售、殆海外銀市於前日電訊、均已報升故金價早市即低、往後買方逾恒、滙　轉佳尤因盛傳我國政擬將改設金本位、或能實行於　遼矣、於是一般投機者、興商彩烈、落手而購、市况突飛孟晋、猛漲十餘兩、竟然再見七百九十六兩之新高峰、治後市因年常舊例、休假無市、今明（十七八日）兩天均亦停市須至十九日照常營業云、

金本位空氣濃騰　自早間四月份開盤七百七十七兩五錢計降三兩六錢因前日大條已升六分之三銀價加四分之一、私電亦加八分之一、繼爲七十七兩、嗣因永　等買進當即高至八十一兩三錢、復後互有一二兩　旋、惟元茂永順利萬興元興永等售出、計貶落二兩、先令揭佈時爲八十兩左右、而滙　掛　已長計英金一二五、美金一二五、日金减一分七五、遂退爲七十九兩三四錢、惟内部逈異三井買六月份二便士、又與朝鮮互做三月花旗二十八元三一二五、而塲内泰康潤宏利志豐永等均有買進、乃價一路進展計漲五六兩旣而英金益緊銀行對做一便士八七五、至十點三刻源成等亦購、激漲　六兩計達九十一兩元茂永等售出回落三兩餘、十一　零計八十七兩半午後復呈高峰、源　元亨等相繼爭購人心更昂、　而上買方甚勁、惟賣者絕少、於是市氣極端俏俐、風　雲　直至午時計達九十六兩然十一點半至十一點三刻、稍有二三兩起仆將屆散市回去一兩迨收盤計爲九十五兩半、比較上週六飛　十四兩四錢、物品做撳五錢、半日間最大價　十六兩、最小價七十七兩、計有十九兩差次、物品早開七十五兩、午收九十五兩、　價已改爲八百五十六兩二錢、計　七十五六兩至六十五六兩、午時僅計六十兩有零、豋賬二　八十六兩、三月八十九兩、四月九十六兩、補水八十六兩、

新年來標紗花一瞥 81

氣象似帶棉荒色彩

人標激漲卅兩左右　標紗自新年紅盤開始以來、步步趨漲、各　價比去歲年底漲起三十兩光景、此種激烈之漲風、初以國府棉紗改　統稅、引動實銷、各帮買去約有七八萬包之巨、底貨抽空、廠商態度强硬、復以金潮淘湧、銀價慘落、以致外棉不能進口、唇齒相關之紗市、因根本上難以鬆動、人心愈堅、而某實業家心　尤濃、吸收不少、空頭方面以原料之飛騰、均呈不穩之狀、市勢愈趨愈高、停市以前雖有數廠套出然仍難减殺買風、空方以日　爲最多於漲風最激烈時、　證金兩大戶解出百餘萬兩前途若何殊不敢預卜也、交易所人標買賣兩方六個　存賬數總成交統計二十一萬二千三百五十包、多頭兩方　過凈成交計七萬四千九百五十包、二月份爲二萬一千五百五十包三月份爲四二千五百五十包四月份五萬零二百包、五月份四萬五千二百五十包、六月份四萬零二百包七月份爲一萬一千七百包、茲將我空兩方買賣　數分誌列後、

漢標高漲十兩　漢標期棉比較去年漲起十兩之　此種情形爲　來所罕見實受匯兌打擊銀價慘落金價狂漲、印棉採算銀盤奇貴、難以進口本國生產之棉自己不　供給外棉不能購定於是投機家大批吸收市盤急　上漲在　市以前頗似有棉荒之虞、空方之恐怖達於極點矣、然世界上生產甚多、但匯兌不鬆、終難來　、所以買方心氣堅决、日商東　洋行購進約有七八萬擔之巨、一般散戶附和者　衆、惟漢帮　賣爲最多損失殊巨、棉市前途、萬難預測也總之存底單薄匯市不長、根本無破綻、交易所成交存賬總計四十七萬零八百擔、多空兩方　直凈計十九萬一千六百擔、二月份爲四萬五千七百擔、三月份爲九萬三千五百擔、四

南洋僑胞極需國貨

上海國貨工廠聯合會、前組織南洋羣島考察團、并推周國鈞爲團長、現各團員業已返國、周君尙因事留汕、昨日周君有長函與該會、報告此行經過及感想、其中所述、於推銷國貨·極有關係、茲特電錄原文如下、逕啟者、國鈞承貴會公推爲南洋　　考察團團長、偕同各團員、南渡三月、由滬出發道經香港法屬　南、去歲十一月二十日抵新加坡、入馬來　邦、達　　、十二月二十三日往　邏、二十八日返　轉往荷　屬蘇門答　·爪哇·今年正月十五日、由新加坡首　反國、除經過情形容返申而爲報告外、謹將考察所得、有關於國產推銷者、略陳其　　、南洋羣島、地居熱帶、氣候和暖、物產豐阜、吾國以歷史關係、地理　　、種植至夥五百萬之南洋僑胞、堅苦耐勞、勤奮儉樸、　南業之牛耳、搓經濟之咽喉、土產之休中販賣、雖外人亦優爲之、然輸入品之内地分銷、則非華僑决無由而實現、僑胞之社會生活狀况、大致仍與國無異、雖數典忘祖之土產、料不盡失其祖傳之生活習慣、故對國貨需要極大、居留南邦之僑胞、其對祖國之熱情、與愛用國貨之熱心、早爲國人所共認、倘祖國工業發達而足以供應南注僑胞、及其他人種之需要、故改良出品、推銷得法、希望實屬無窮、去歲土　　跌、一落千丈、爲向來所未見、破產時聞、失業日增然輸入方面則因殖民地經濟落後、生活程度較低、巨爲原料出產地、日用所需、多仰給外來、而銷耗之貨品、尤少貴重之奢侈品、多數皆爲日用所必需、故　在恐慌之中、購買力弱、然欲不消費仍不可能、加以金貴銀賤、及僑胞愛用國貨之熱烈可佩、國貨對南之推銷决不因南洋之貿易衰落、而受極大之影響、且爲推銷之良機、查我國對南貿易不振之主要原因、有二、（一）則以中國尙在原料供給於人之地位、（二）則以華僑社會之生活内容、不盡與祖國同、而國内製造家、亦未能順應其需要、而爲　當之供給、是以　入南洋之國貨、除食品及農品外、繼製國貨、不過差强人意、故銷行之貨、向以雜貨爲大宗、雜貨種類至繁屈指難數、其最幌銷於市塲者、若山貨·即竹　·衣　·竹椅·等　器是、若生油·雜糧·神　·紙料·海味·烟茶·　器·鮮　·菜蔬·等爲數不鮮、機製國貨其則除紙烟·毛巾·線　·線襪·衣料·等製品、間有若干銷於土人、或其他　民社會外、餘均専供數百萬華僑之消息、夫人之謀我者、使用政治手段、行其經濟侵略、以前者爲先　、後者爲依歸、吾國地大物博、惜不能取而出之、工業落後、較他人有望　莫及、　　莫塞、利　外　、渴望國内外同胞、振興工業、改良製品、以我樂用國貨·富有　買力之五百萬華僑爲後援、溝通中南商業、發　國外貿易、協力赴之、我對南輸出貿易、不難與日俱增、可斷言也、先此佈逵、餘容陸續報告云云、

拒毒會呈請中央制止鴉片公賣 89

公賣非屬無因

應請嚴厲制止

中華國民拒毒會、以鴉片　賣、近來各方傳聞、甚　塵上、特聯合各關係團體、極力抗爭、業已疊誌前報、日前、該會名譽主席唐少川、召集常務委員會議、討論應会辦法、决議、呈請中央電部、　據總理遺訓、訓令國府禁烟常局、切實禁絕烟毒、並訓令各地黨部、禁止鴉片公賣之宣傳、以重烟禁、茲慄錄其原呈如次、呈爲呈請根據總理遣訓、嚴厲禁絕鴉片、並宣傳制止公賣事、竊以鴉片流毒、爲禍無窮、總理拒毒遺訓、有謂鴉片營業、絕對不能與人民所賦予權力之國民政府兩立、又云、苟有主張法律准許鴉片營業者、均爲民意之公敵、苟負責之政府機關、爲自身之私便、對鴉片下旗息戰、不問外暫苠

均屬賣國之行爲等語、國民黨黨綱、對於禁絕鴉片之政策、料有明白之規定、本會遵總理之遺訓、秉承本黨之黨網、發軔拒毒運動、奮鬥未敢稍懈、幸於北伐完成之時、促成政府實施禁絕政策、不意近得各方傳言、禁烟黨局、對於完全禁絕之政策、有所變更、現已籌備施行全國公賣、雖經中央禁烟委員會聲明不確、而外間傳聞紛紜、咸謂證據鑿鑿、且謂江海關某客卿、已承某當局之委託、正在起草公賣鴉片章程、完全以籌欵爲目的、每年預算收入在八千萬元至一萬萬元、財部又派前時辦理鴉片公賣最力之李基鴻等、馳赴台灣、調查當地鴉片公賣　度、準備仿行、引起當地華僑之反對、而現任中央禁烟委員會委員長劉瑞恒、向日日社記者之談話、亦未　白否認、甚且赴台調查公賣之李基鴻、與公然主張公賣之伍連德、均經正式任命、爲中央禁烟委員會委員、是則禁烟當局、採取公賣之政策、已在着着進行中、　以絕對禁絕鴉片政策、國府旣有　白頒佈、昭示全國、中外咸知、雖年來各地奉行未力、如兩湖鴉片特稅、粵桂公開賣土、川閩雲貴種烟、爲國人所詬病、然完全禁絕之政策、固不可因此而稍示游移也、苟禁烟當局、言行相違、承認鴉片爲一種法律所許可之營業、是不特違背前此所頒佈之禁烟法、且亦違國民黨黨綱、違背國際條約、違背總理遺訓、本會從事拒毒、素以發揮民衆願望爲責職、對此禍國殃民之辦法、深爲不可、最近四中全會舉行之時、黨國諸公、復有厲行烟禁之决議、今如一旦施行公賣、國譽民生、行將不堪設想、本會心所謂危、　安煘默、理合　情上陳、懇請鈞部、訓令國府禁烟常局、　實禁絕烟毒、責令取銷兩湖特稅處、以及粵桂公賣禁烟局等機關、而對於各地鴉片公賣者之宣傳、尤請訓令全國各級黨部、嚴行制止、以正觀聽而維黨綱、一方面以訂定拒毒工作、爲各地黨部進行中主要　之事功、以促民衆之注意、而增烟禁之實力、迫切陳詞、乞爭諒察、謹呈中國國民黨中央執行委員會、

伍連德致拒毒會函 90

伍連德博士昨函中華國民拒毒會云、逕啟者查貴會前未徵伍連德同意、即以歷名　入執行委員之列、正以拒毒事務、人同此心、而亦切符連德之素志也、故並汪以冒昧處事相　責、乃此後貴會對内對外等一切會務、迄未見貴會有來函通知、而　各文件則轉有　名列入、亦正所以同列、　諸公、均皆一時碩彥、而所曾事項又爲萬衆一心之「　　」也、因变未加深察而聽之、連德近因鑒於鴉片與麻醉品之流　不特我中國受其害、近且迷漫於全球、又復承中外有心人之不吝下詢、囑擬禁烟之澈底辦法、以供大家商量、目擊心傷之餘、何容老而不　以固辭、爰就數十年　見所及、發表「流専已極之　片問題」文、純爲余個人意見、供國人之研究與考慮、並非代表任何機關團體之主砦更非　貢於當局乃人所共應研究之問題中一種意見耳、目的在期望將烟　　底禁絕、毌再徒勞　簧之舌、而任令烟　之日見增盛也、不謂竟　貴會不諒、厚誣連德以主張鴉片公賣云云、竊思連德對於我國受害最烈之鴉片毒物、早已視爲我中華民族之奇心恥巨敵、故於禁烟問題、悉心研究、已數十年、當否雖不敢必、然絕非徒憑搖旗呐喊如　子之弄把戲、亦非表心病狂含有不可告人之驻隱、以求干進者可比、蓋凡欲達到事實之止的、不能僅在直線上呆觀、必先平心靜氣、研究一切實辦法始爲功、况余所著文中、通篇也　不着半個公賣字樣、讀貴會宣言、「伍連德公然在報上主張實行鴉片公賣」云云、不知究何所據、誠恐因訛傳　誤、何以使得、昨晤貴會所稱名舉主席唐少川先生、據謂十三日臨時常務會議、初請唐先生到會、而遭其拒絕、繼則由貴會總幹事黃嘉惠君等三數人遷就其居茶話、黃君頗多不公道言語、大有束縛連德言論自由之氣槪、頻經唐先生加以糾正之、是唐行狂對於黃君言動、已示不满、嗣又散見各報、大　名譽主席唐某某、議决提案七八條云云、貴會宗旨、在拒毒、聽令　列　名、感　各界之助力不少、豈知英稄更事如黃君、將玩置　成於常上乎、嗚呼、連德服勞祖國、幾三十年、痛心疾首於鴉片問題、而加以研究之時間者亦如之、祖以事　絕難専顧、致不克於拒毒一途、有所建樹、即治標辦法、如予烟民戒烟機會之戒烟醫院、亦至今未見設立、豪强種販、直視而束手無策、年耗鉅資於拒毒聲中、而互氛汎濫於全國者如故、拘衷自問、能毌愧作、連德報國有心、而兩　已霜、但　於老當益壯之訓、則　未敢示弱、然人各有志、未能强同、如後生可畏之黃君嘉惠、則吾又何敢再與同儕乎、爲特泐　奉佈、請貴會即日起、不准再用　名、列入於執行委員名義、免　觀聽而清黑白、相應函達、即希查照爲　、此致中華國民拒毒會、伍連德啟、二十、二、十六、

市商會呈報木器油漆業組織糾紛 107

無進行調解可能

市商會昨爲中西木器號業·與油漆業·組織糾紛呈報社會局曁民　會云、呈爲呈復事案於本年一月十六日、奉社會局第五八零二號令内開、案據中西木器號、業公會呈爲油漆公會派人向木器號、求入會請糾正並附會章及徵求入會啟各一份等情、據此查據稱各　是否屬實事關的業糾紛合行檢發　呈令仰該會遵照、迅即查明、秉公糾正具報察奪等因附發原　呈一件、會章及徵求入會啟、各一份到會並於一月三十日奉民訓會同前因飭即迅行派員查明調處具報等因查此事　奉社會局訓令後即經派員調查據中西木器號業公會聲稱　加入油漆業之泡力水帮、係　作塲與西式木器號有　客之别、所谓内作之木器嫁粧　店則係中　木署店之油漆作蓋一木器號必附股漆作其加入團體、　隨主體之训方爲標　、詢其加入該會之木器號　數、則稱西式木器號二十九家中式木器號　家、又據油漆業同業公會聲稱、該會係招牌油漆及油漆輪船之外作及油漆木器嫁粧之内作、發起建造、光緒二十三年油漆汽車馬車帮捐資加入民國八年、加入油漆圓作帮民國十年、加入油漆小件等六帮、集合而成、民國十五年、由上海縣商會召集六帮代表、捐購滬南基地一處呈准前上海縣、發給布告、自奉令改組後、所謂中西木器號　、亦均已包括在内、訽其木器號加入者究有若干、則稱、中式木器號幾全部加入西式木器號則不足十家當以該兩業情形、旣如上述、即於一月二十九日召集該兩業、各派代表來會、聽候調解、其時油漆業爲過去歷史關係堅持合併組織中西木器號業則以主體各異性質不同、未願　併遂由　會提出調解意見略謂、就業務性質而言、油漆業係於所售物品上加工製造之一種工程、自不能以加工製造之工程而包含其主體之　業、故中西木器號　應加入中西木器號、業公會惟油漆業　有資產、其一部分由中西木器號、業捐資　置、强欲令其脫離油漆業而加入木器業旣與雙方無益、徒滋引起糾紛中式木器號之加入木器業公會旣僅有三家而西式木器業之加入油漆業公會者亦不足十家、不如將中西木器號業公會逕改爲西式木器號　業公會將加入該會中式木器號　家改入油漆同業公會、而將加入油漆同業公會之泡力水帮會員、與西式木器號　性質令其加入中西木器號業公會以　　限、否則、果如中西木器業　　每一木器號必附設漆作、則令漆作部份加入油漆業同業公會、木器部分加入中西木器號、業公會以資解决、商議之餘該兩　調解辦法、兩業均未挅納、遂無結果而散、嗣又奉民訓會令將本案查明調處具報爱續訂於二月十日再行調解、詎屆時、中西木器號業公會、具　一函以雖承召集、必無良好結果等語、拒絕出席屬會以情勢至此、認爲已無進行調解之可能理合將奉文遵辦經過情形、呈報鈞局鑒核、至屬會所擬調解兩種辦法、有無可以酌採、

爲將來本案解决參考之處伏候鈞裁云、

饒伯森將演講空氣 108

本埠靑年協會科學演講部幹事饒伯森博士、爲美國著名科學家、每年在吾國各地演講科學問題、　用　製之儀器、　明聲光力電各項物理科學上之基本原理、故每至一處、各界人士無不朋加歡迎、博士爲中國靑年會服務已二十有八年將於今春返美、茲定於本月廿四五六等日、在靑年協會演講廳、舉行特别演講三日、束邀各界友人聽講、作爲臨别紀念、此次演講總題爲「空氣之潤澤性、」白分子之吸引作用、大至天體之旋轉運行、無不包羅在内、並有奇巧之儀器爲助、令聽者易於明　、聆此一席話、勝讀一部科學書也、

女學生自殺 121

張鏡如神思恍惚

胡範若注意周全

情人槍敎案屬奇離

南火車站大同大學内女學生張鏡如特於昨日上午十時許、在該校宿舍内、用利刃自刎、當由該校發覺後、立即車送上海醫院醫治、不料因受傷過重、延至十一時許殞命、茲將所得詳情、錄之於下、

入學經過　徐州人張次書者、住居作州沛縣帽舖街西首、生兩子三女、最幼之女即係鏡如、現年十九歲、姿態秀麗、性情寡默、前年鏡如因乃兄道源、在上海大同大學内大學部讀書、鏡如亦即獨自來滬、赴該校投考後、得入初中肄業、而平日對於師生及同學之間、均甚相得、光陰荏苒、轉瞬一學期已畢、鏡如遂束裝返里去後、不知何故、至下學期開學時、鏡如不到該校、而校中師長疑其轉入他校肄業、故亦一在意中、本年二月一日、大同大學開學之期、校長曹惠君忽接郵遞書信一封、展視後、始知由張鏡如所寄來、内中所云、要求重行入校、惟不知再考與否、特來詢問、當時曹校長以鏡如係舊學生、若重入初中年級、則可免予考試、乃就去函答復、至五日、鏡如果係帶行李等來校、除照例繳納學費後該校即以舊學生資格辦理、不令其塡寫保證書等、一面即爲指定在十九號宿舍内居住、　　稱病延醫　本月六日全體校生俱行上課、獨鏡如則臥於宿舍、終日不出、直至次晨、始行上課、但同學等亦皆未見其他異狀、至九日下午、鏡如忽患頭痛、欲請假半天、當經敎師胡範若允許、鏡如即步入宿舍、入榻安臥、至十日上午、鏡如又向胡師請求續假半天、即便至校外醫院内就醫、胡以出外就醫、亦係尋常之事故即允予續假、鏡如乃欣然出校、比至十一時許回校、逕入宿舍内、其同宿舍之同學、俱向埀詢醫治後如何、鏡如稱由醫生打了一針後、身體稍覺好些、現將服藥了、同學聞之、即代倒開水、鏡如堅拒、後自行取開水一杯、面對玻窗、將藥呑下、然同學等咸未悉其所吃者究係何種藥品、鏡如服藥之後、即行安睡、下午亦未上課、至旁晚時、胡異而親赴宿舍、探視鏡如之病狀、但睹鏡如精神極感疲瘁、按其脈息、似有似無、知係病勢轉劇、遂急用電話請蔡醫師前來診視後、亦不明其病由、

送入醫院　十一日髰　恐發生危險、立將鏡如車送上海醫院診治後、仍不知其所患何病、惟見其精神困疲、故急打强心針一針、入夜始見其精神少振、至十二日、胡以其病牂奇特、乃復入其宿舍内察看有無異狀、偵視良久、忽在窗沿上發現安神藥水空瓶一只、而窗外又發現安神藥片空盒一只、始知鏡如委係服毒自殺、並非疾病、於是急即函召其家屬來申、一面赶往上海醫院、報告醫師之後、立即設法救療、至晚間鏡如堅欲回校、該院因其毒藥已經設法打出、可告無恙、遂許其返校、鏡如已返校、

周媽看護　胡恐再發生變故、乃雇一傭婦周媽、専爲服侍、间囑注意監視一切、至十三日、胡又去面詢其因何自殺之原因、因鏡如謂有一同學、心思最毒、要想報仇、我竟爲了他蒙了不白之寃、這是惡社會所造成、我自殺之念、你是我的親愛之敎師、萬望嚴守秘密、不可將我服毒之情形、宣布於人、胡慨然允許、至十四日、胡又往探視時、鏡如取給洋三十二元、託胡存其校中、並將書就一封書信、更託代爲寄遞、信内大旨以我今病已就痊、請其家長不必來申、並擬再行轉入他校等等、胡恐再發生事故、乃將原函收藏、至十五日（前日）清晨六時許、鏡如忽步入胡之臥室、要求給假、以便出外醫病、胡令暫緩、而彼竟悻悻而出、未幾、鏡如得悉原信未寄、特遣周媽前支索回、

刎頸殞命　至昨日上午十時許、周媽忽急遽奔告胡謂、不好了、一好了、胡尙疑鏡如或發生疾病、乃赶入宿舍密視、當揭啓床帳、但見鏡如手中尙握小洋刃一柄、满沾鮮血、頸項間亦有鮮血汨汨流出、床帳已染殷紅之血、始悉其自刎、不禁大駭、遂急備車送往上海醫院、延至十一時許竟已香消玉殞矣、事爲該管一區一分所得悉、立飭二十三舖地甲秦德芳、報請上海地方法院相騐、其屍體已由該校舁回校中、

北平南來謀事未成

受人挑撥與妻離異

百感叢集服毒自裁

北方無可生活　於十七年　擋得資七千元、　同姨妹來滬、營謀職業、抵滬後、借寓閘北寳興路協興里一○五號沈命三（前廣東造幣廠任事）家樓下、找前上海市長張定　謀事未成、在滬以所帶之欵借放、收取利息生活、其小姨認沈夫婦爲義父母、詎被沈夫婦挑撥、致吳夫妻口角失和、吳之

小姨不外病殁　而吳之金錢、除陸續借出千餘金、執有票據外、餘者多被人編借凈盡、至此、吳夫婦感情、愈趨惡劣、於上年廢曆七月間、由沈等居間協議離婚、姚氏以胞妹已死、

Page 12

世界小事記 134

·海·客

英美大都會中。有幾家大洗衣店。對於洗滌領圈一項。前後計有十七種手續之多。

英國以裝設海底電綫著名的船「法闌台」”FARAAAY“曾於四十八年間裝設海底電綫五萬英里。現在已退休了。

人力車最初創行於日本。故俗稱東洋車。據一九二三年一月調查所得。日本在二十二年以前。有人力車三十萬輛。通行市上。年來逐漸减少。現存不到十萬輛。

英國新發明一種寒暑表。比一隻男子所用的時計略大。裏面裝有特别的法條。隨著天氣的改變、冷時能降到冰點以下十度。熱時能升到一百三十度。

英國最著名的歌劇「乞兒行」。曾經表演過九百九十八次。内中的演員都係原班人物。唱白熟極而流。從未錯誤。不料在第九百九十九次表演時。内中有一個伶人忽然忘了他所應說的話。大家都以爲奇事。

歐洲飛行事業。一在發達一天、最近有人製造一種小飛機。每小時可飛四十英里。内容駕駛員一人與旅客一人的座位。所費每架祇須一百五十金鎊。

孫寳琦軼事 135

馬·一·笠·

先生字慕韓。晚年别署孟晉老人。武陵望族也。歷任顯宦。並出使外洋。在政五十載。煊赫三十年。黨國底定。始引退南下。卜居海上。膝下兒女衆多。境狀奇窘。蓋先生生平樂善好施。且不擅經濟學。以致服務多載。仍兩袖清風。家無擔石。月前因病留滬。遽歸道山。噩耗傳來。凡識與不識。莫不同聲嗟惋。予世受鴻恩。無以相報。爲文至此。不禁感愧交併。爰摭述其軼事數則。藉以風世。而表彰先生德行之萬一云爾。

甲子齊盧戰爭。先生爲桑梓請命。隻身奔走。幾無虚日。旋联前線已實行開　。迺嘆息不置。盧子嘉召讌督署先生竟撕去請柬。遠走湖濱。次晨偕同避難民衆離杭。無一知者。

翌年孫馨遠入浙。適門下士夏超主省政。夏因擴充警備。爲孫部忌。漸起暗潮。各自戒備。形勢緊張。如王竹齊金百順輩。共起週旋無效。卒推先生出。時正嚴冬。更深夜靜。尙在軍署中作揖道歉。其能不忘故鄕安危。有是者。洵難能也。

先生敦尙古道。天性至孝。介弟仲璵亦然。璵名寳瑄。曾任甬海關監督。第逢春秋，必相偕歸里。探親掃墓。來則必寓其先岳張勤果公祠。祠本饒風景。幽雅精潔。頗宜小住。昆仲遇無酬酢。輒相携游湖。某年月夜。擬放棹三潭。苦無舟子。適予與先兄文彬在側。自告奮勇。分任打槳職。浩蕩前進。先生昆仲亦捲袖相助。破風逐浪。逸興遄飛。往事猶歷歷在目。撫今追昔。能不悵然。

民黨鉅子蔣觀雲先生病故滬寓。先生扶杖送殯號哭里許。淚跡甫乾。喪報又臨。其六妹張夫人罹疾去世。星夜奔往。撫柩慟哭。三日内老淚頻揮。目瀋枯竭其於故人情感之深。似有非常人所可及者。　　黨軍出師。先生引退南下。黨國要人。咸多稱頌。或詢以孫總理主義如何。彼必翹其母指稱曰「好」。並稱本人與總理友交甚篤。對蔣總司令尤多誇讚。如遇國事。類多關懷。浙省府張靜江曾聘爲高等顧問。時有貢獻。故先生之於黨國。亦不無微勞也。

雪 136

秋·水·

這幾天來。上海連朝大雪。眞正好看煞人。俗云。冬雪保五榖。春雪保人口。現在我們旣有冬雪。復有春雪。那末好看之外。更屬可喜的了。

然而雪這種東西。就目前而論。則有害而無益。尤其在交能一方面。雪本視爲交通四大仇之首。何謂四大仇。一雪、二霧、三雹、四水。霧能迷途。雹毀車輛。水没規轍。均爲交能之大敵。而雪於迷失途程。毀損車輛。淹没規轍之外。又來一個壓毀電線。你想雪之爲患又如何。

火車見雪。更屬棘手。猶憶一八六六年。英國之北數地NORTHNUMBERLAND大雪。積高至五六尺。火車幾全埋入雪中。旣不能行動。車中客更没法出外。交通人員設法除雪。方把車客救出。然而有一部分人則守候至四日之久。雪消方得出車。眞正可怕

因此。在歐美各國的鐵路局裏。必有特製之除雪車設備。除雪車以鋼質或木料造成。爲重至少須二十六號。有輪三對。以機發動。輪旁更有鐵板及鐵刷數事。雪

中或雪後。沿鐵軌一路開去。能把積雪推向左右。把鐵軌洗刷乾凈。車内有火爐以取暖。有廚房以製飲食。可容數十人。因爲雪後沿途除雪。輒須費一二日之繼續工作啊。

英國的腦福克。於一八八一年。遭未有之大雪。其地火車當然不能開行。而除雪車亦難聽命。因爲雪下得太大。天氣又冷。除雪車的引擎小。就没法可想。最後借用八個火車龍頭。在車後生火推去。方得開動。亦雪中一件趣事。

十三爲吉數 137

志·政

鄭寳照與十三

京滬滬柿甬　兩路車務處長鄭揚生（寳照）氏。爲我國有數之鐵道専家。精幹練達。治事尤勤。嘗與先生閒談。先生謂十三一數。西國人士。多目爲不祥。然與予則殊有意外緣。猶憶予之加入萬國儲蓄會。數載以來。從未獲獎。予亦淡然置之久矣。詎知某日該會突送來大洋數百元。曰。此中得之獎金也。予驚且喜。視案上日歷。赫然十三號也。亦云巧矣。

誌謝與介紹　褚民誼先生主編之醫藥評論。發行業已兩年。以宣傳醫藥常識討論衛生設施爲宗旨。價値之高。一時無兩。昨承贈二周　念　　介紹金石名家　揚州黃君漢侯。爲近代金石名家。尤擅刻扇。眞草篆隸。以及諸家書法。臨摹無不畢肖。所刻扇骨。長不逾尺寬。僅數分。有刻前後赤璧賦或前後出師表者。有寫全部聖敎或全部蘭亭及十三跋者。呼仿其體。神韻不爽。秀潤葱倩。細若蚊足。目力稍鈍者。非以顯微鏡不能詳　。上海各大　扇莊均有漢侯作品。其潤格並不過昂。可逕向揚州多子街　大莊黃君處函索。謹爲介紹。以告同好。

書報介紹

靑萍月刋創刋號 140

湯·彬·

杭州的文藝界、最近是異常勃興、是一般愛好文藝的、靑年所組織的小規模的文藝團體、也大都有定期刋物的發行、而且它底内容、都是屬於提倡民族主義文藝的、這實是中國内地文藝界一種良好的現象、其原因、無疑地是受了海上民族主義文藝運動的影響、我們要曉得、近代的中國文學是缺乏一種正確的中心思想、所以使整個的文藝界弄得黑漆一團、思想的混亂、實不可以言語形容、最有碍於靑年們的光明的前途的、莫如在不久以前盛興一時的那普羅文藝了、如果我們要肅清這些腐化和惡化的思想、那只有鼓吹一種靑年們所需要的具有心思想的文藝、在無形中那種不正確的思想就會洗清的了、

民族主義文藝運動成爲中國文壇的主潮、就是爲了它具有確的中心思想、而且這是爲目前靑年界所最需要的、我們　要看民族主義文藝自海上發動以來、各地的刋物和報章所響應的却不在少數、這發現於杭州文藝界的「靑萍月刋」、就是其中最有力的一種、

這創刋號的内容、頗爲豐富、如丁淚鴻的「狂奏着吧」、徵波的「民族性文學與人生、」和幽微底「心曲」、曉風的「像樣的紳士、」公助的「你怎能盡情地留戀、」没名的「爲了不忠實」、徘霞的一咱們的世界」等、都是値得注意的力作、至少在思想上是具有正確的意識的、

在「我們的開端」裏、是這樣的在狂奏着、「我們抓住了時代、這時代在我們生命的節奏上佔着很重要的一段、但、朋友、你當記着、這是很容易過去了的、也要、會像已往死黯底年華一般地消逝、在四週的無形的、在虚渺的幻想中、牠輕輕地消逝了、因此、我們需要在這裏對人生下一個深刻的認識、然後如此平凡地記錄着、這認識是極廣義的、是我們生活的小模型、是我們呐喊的收音機、···我們要記錄着、記錄着這些平凡的故事、同時、把内心的美妙底顏色顯示出來、作我們靈魂生存上的一個紀念、因了這點極微小極微小的意思、靑萍的蓓蕾今天開始展着了、隨着我們又接受新的命運之神底啓示、依賴着花的鮮艷嬌嫩、去完成一切、同情我們的朋友們、請站在我們同一的陣線上、彈響心弦、盡力地狂奏着吧、趁着靑春、來負起這使命、」

在引起我們感動的狂奏之後、就是一篇有力的論著丨民族性文學與人生、内容雖然嫌單簡一些、但是所論各點都很正確的、

同時、作者對於中國的文壇亦有評判、這也很確實的話、如他所述、「我們看中國的新文壇是呈顯着怎樣的現象、自從十幾年前轟轟烈烈的閙着新文學運動以來、其間固然有不少活潑的情感、以實現爲題材的作品以來、然而到現在新文學並不見怎樣的一日千里、精神異常銷沉、」這當然、它最大的缺點還是爲了没有正確的中心思想、使中國的新文藝不能有所發展、我們要拯救中國文壇的危機、即是使新文學有所的表現、那麽、非提倡民族主義文藝不可了、在作者、也想到了這一點、所以最後他是這樣的結束着、「現在是二十世紀了、我們應負起這時代、所需要的文學、丨民族主義文學丨底使命、」這般靑年者、如果這樣的來努力、一定能夠得到偉大的收果、但是現在已經有了相當的成績突現於我們的眼前了、

「像樣的紳士、」「和爲了不忠實」兩篇小說、都値得我們一讀、因爲他們見解都是非常正確的、實際我們也可以把它當作理想的文字看、在詩歌方面、尤其是一些珍貴的作品、有豐富的情感、向上的意識美麗的字句、鼓勵的雋語、因爲篇幅關係、在此怒不一一加以徵引了、

在杭州的文藝界、能給我們這樣的有力的一種提倡民族主義文學的刋物給我們、委實是可喜的現象、而且、他們在萌芽的時代、就有這樣蓬勃的生氣、以後的開展、當然是無可限量的呢、我熱誠的在此作愼重的推薦、却是極有意義的事吧、最後、我希望「靑萍」同人發奮努力、希望海上文藝界對他們有所注意、

靑年園地

從醫院回去 141

安·娜·

一個冰天雪地的下午

一路電車、那顆粒般的雪花、有了北風的鞏助、格外來得活潑的在空中飛舞、我雖然披上了大衣和戴上了帽子、也敵不過他的攻擊、心裏愈是着急、電車愈是姗姗來遲、害得我面上像有千萬枚針刺着般的作　、

陰暗的天、更顯出他的困倦了、路燈漸漸增多了、我念着家人的企望着我、尤其是母親的遠念呀、她會在這漸入黃昏的當兒、冒風雪的立在門前、伸長了頸子在等待着她那外出求學的兒女回家、她度日如年的望着、眉間的皺紋漸漸增多了呵、偉大的母愛、會使困倦了的遊子的必靈舒快、使充满了煩愁的人們都會微笑的、使我這冰凍了的身軀溫暖······

呵、偉大的母愛、

這樣的想着、微笑着、彷佛已立在母親的跟前、看到她慈祥的容顏和那和藹的慰問、忘却了自己還立在這雪地之上、手中還有一包方才在醫院解剖下來的胎兒的心心臟、肺臟、和肝臟、

這胎兒不幸横產、在子宮内經過了長久時期而　死了、他還得了梅梅毒的遺傳、丨由肝臟的肥大告訴我的、他生得很好看、像熟睡了的嬰孩、雙頰還像萍菒般紅得可愛、我不相信他是離開了人間的人、是没靈魂的人、唉、我不知怎的、對這可愛無辜的胎兒、表十二分憐憫的同情、　　··················

開始解剖了、那閃光的刀在他腹部

1931.02.17

Wang Jinyu's Troops Defeat Bandit Stronghold in Pingxiang 1

He Bandit Still Flees to Shihe

(Changsha) Liu Jianxu telegraphed that Kong Bandit attempted to invade Pingjiang, with a detachment disturbing eastern Yue. Additional troops from Peng's division and Liu's brigade were dispatched to Pingjiang to assist in the suppression. The bandits who fled Chaling will retreat to the Gan border. Wang Jinyu's troops defeated the bandit stronghold in Wugong Mountain, Pingxiang. (14th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) He telegraphed Jiang, stating that various bandit suppression units restored political training offices and are seriously clearing the countryside. (15th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) He approved Guangxin's seven counties' request, ordering Ruan Zhaochang to suppress Fang Bandit in Yushan. (15th Dispatch)

(Changsha) Li Jue arrived in the province on the 15th to discuss border defense in the Hunan-Hubei border area. Zhang Ying returned to Anxiang on the 17th. Liu Jianxu went to eastern Pingjiang to arrange border defenses. (16th Dispatch)

(Changsha) He Yingqin telegraphed He Jian, ordering a team to take over the defense of Pingxiang, and dispatching Wang Jinyu's troops and Luo Guanying's division to pursue the bandits. (15th Dispatch)

(Changsha) Wang Dongyuan went to Pingdong Changshou to suppress Kong Bandit. Chen Quzhen telegraphed that He Bandit was intercepted but still fled to Shihe. Spanish Imperial System Barely Surviving 32

Royal Family Abuses Privileges, Popular Grievances Boil Over

Republican Forces激[Excited]张[Increase], Overall Trend Gone

King Calls on Leader of Liberal Party to Form Cabinet

Reuters, Madrid, 15th - The people of Spain are extremely agitated, especially in the capital and major industrial cities. Demonstrations continue throughout the day, and explicitly demand the king's abdication and the abolition of the imperial system. They are no longer satisfied with amending the constitution, and cries for the king's early death can be heard from time to time. On one occasion, a large group of people attempted to attack the prison to release those detained in the recent revolutionary case, but were eventually dispersed by the police and security forces. The situation in cities outside the capital such as Zaragoza, Barcelona, Valencia, Granada, Seville, and other major towns is the same. In short, the republican forces have spread everywhere. The main question at the moment is when the army will join the revolution, but most people believe that this will also happen very soon.

Reuters, Madrid, 15th - Campo arrived here today and, after meeting with the King, conferred with General Berenguer at the Ministry of War on everything. Campo later issued an article saying that he advised the King to accept a government organized by the left wing. The King has now telegraphed Alba, the leader of the Liberal Party who is living in Paris, urging him to return to Beijing immediately. It is likely that the King will ask Alba to form a cabinet. General public opinion favors a complete amendment to the constitution and a reduction of the King's power. From the looks of it, the King is now willing to obey the extreme left wing. Berenguer told people that he denied the claim that he would go abroad for rest. He wants to stay a little longer to find a suitable position in the army.

Reuters, Paris, 15th - Spanish Liberal Party leader Alba did not give a definitive statement tonight when reporters asked him about the King's telegram urging him to return to the country, but said that he would have to wait until the King agreed to amend the inherited policies of the Spanish monarchy before he could return to Mali. Alba received the King's telegram asking him to return to the country immediately yesterday, and it is expected that the King will ask him to form a cabinet. Alba previously fled from Spain to Paris as a political exile.

Reuters, Madrid, 15th - Catallón leader Campo wrote to a newspaper, saying that what the country needs is neither a dictatorial vocabulary nor a revolution, let alone the maintenance of the current political system, but only to be ruled by true democracy. Reuters, Madrid, 15th - Minor disturbances occurred in various places here yesterday. The Republican Party did not listen to the official ban and held meetings in many places. The police dispersed them repeatedly. The King received many political leaders today, each telling the King his opinions on the future government.

Reuters, Berlin, 15th - The Berlin Daily's Madrid correspondent commented on the Berenguer government, stating that since Berenguer succeeded Rivera as Prime Minister on January 29 last year, he called for the elimination of the abuses of dictatorship and the restoration of the constitutional rights of popular sovereignty as soon as Congress abolished the laws announced by the Rivera government. And because the Liberal Party承[Taking]六年[Six Years]推[Push]克[Conquer]狄[Di](or Dick)多[Many]政[Government]之后[After], if the freely elected Congress is convened suddenly, it seems too dangerous for the royal family, so Berenguer had to extend the election period again and again, first trying to restore royal power. However, the general trend has gone, even the most severe inspection system cannot slightly hinder the activities of the Republican faction. Because of this, newspapers and leaflets criticizing the people in power filled the country, and the king was the center of public resentment. The group pointed out that he abused his privileges, plundered the people's wealth to enrich himself privately, and transported huge amounts of money abroad for safety, while forcing the people of the country to keep money in the country, suffering losses from devaluation. Words of such resentment are too numerous to list, resulting in popular grievances boiling over and the loss of all popular support. In addition, the people around the king are all taking care of their own interests and not thinking about preserving the throne at all, so today the Spanish imperial system has reached the end of the road. Its hope of maintaining its unfallen state is almost exhausted.

Jiji News Agency, Tokyo, 16th - After the Japanese Metropolitan Police Department举[Lift]日本[Japan]共产[Communist]党[Party] (the so-called 4.16 case), it learned of a secret society of Chinese students studying in Japan organizing the Chinese Communist Party and its plans to expand its party organization nationwide with Tokyo as the center. Recently, as the relationship between the Chinese and Japanese governments came to an end, the ban was lifted at 5 PM today. After Police Commissioner General Maruyama visited Chinese Minister Wang Rongbao to request understanding, he arrested them all at dawn the next day. Earlier, on August 4, Showa 4, the Metropolitan Police Department learned that there were more than 100 Chinese students studying in Japan plotting to destroy the Chinese Embassy in a vacant lot near the Matsuya Department Store in Ginza, Tokyo. It immediately ordered the entire police force of the Kitakanya Police Station to be dispatched, and 14 chief instigators were arrested and sentenced to 29 days of detention. As a result of the serious interrogation, the secret organization of the Chinese Communist Party was discovered. The Communist Party members established Communist Party branches in Sendai, Sapporo, Yokohama, Kyoto, Okayama, Nagasaki, etc., and contacted each other, planning to promote the organization and attempt to redden the East. Current Affairs Commentary

New Trends in the Spanish Political Situation 34

The resignation of the Spanish cabinet this time is not a problem of the cabinet itself, but a problem of whether the imperial system should存[Survive]废[Be Abolished] or not. If the problem is of the cabinet itself, and the successor is elected well, the political situation can be stabilized. If the problem is of the imperial system and affects the cabinet, then unless a real solution is obtained on the two paths of monarchy and democracy, the cabinet is reorganized and the political situation will eventually be unstable. The Spanish have long wanted a republic and unanimously advocated that the King of Spain must abdicate. However, the King of Spain still wants to maintain his position and is anxiously looking for a successor. But those who are slightly aware of the situation dare not take on this important task of transition. Therefore, as we measure it, the future situation will not go beyond two paths. One is to amend the constitution to reduce the power of the king, and the other is to revise the new constitution and implement a democratic system. The first theory is advocated by the general moderates, and the second theory is advocated by the radicals and the majority of the people. In the future, the King of Spain will have no choice but to follow the first theory and allow the amendment of the constitution. As Liberal Party leader Alba said today, he must wait until the King of Spain agrees to amend the powers of the Spanish monarch before he can respond to the King's invitation and return to China. Only in this way can Alba's return to China and the formation of a cabinet perhaps ease the situation for a time. However, this policy of easing the situation for a time cannot挽回[Restore] the hearts of those who advocate thorough reform. Look at the words of Catalan leader Campo, who said that what Spain needs today is neither a dictatorial system, nor a meaningless revolution, nor the maintenance of the current political system, but only to obtain the rule of true democracy. These words are enough to represent the hearts of the general Spanish people. Therefore, simply amending the constitution and reducing royal power will never satisfy the Spanish people. Therefore, unless the goal of democratic politics is fully achieved and the second theory is implemented, the Spanish republican movement will never stop for a day, and the political situation will never be stable. This is a prediction that can only be made.

Indian Dandi People Continue to Destroy Salt Law 35

Reuters, Surat, 15th - It is heard that Dandi, where Gandhi first broke the Salt Law, has now had a popular movement of non-violent resistance. Twenty-one tons of salt from the salt fields there were taken away by the people.

Sino-American Negotiations on the Issue of Extraterritoriality 36

Washington, 15th (Associated Press dispatch) – State Department officials today continued discussions with Dr. Wu Chaoshu, the Chinese Minister to Washington, regarding China's request for the abolition of extraterritorial rights enjoyed by American citizens in China. It is reported that the current point of contention lies in the matter of foreign advisory judges in Chinese courts. The Chinese side strongly advocates that after the abolition of consular jurisdiction, foreigners may serve in Chinese courts in an advisory capacity, but even this should be of a temporary nature. The American side, however, insists that foreign judges must be permanently stationed in Chinese courts, and that foreign personnel should be able to step in and replace Chinese judges when the latter are unable to render impartial verdicts. It is heard that during the recent exchange of views in Washington, a compromise solution was discussed. The United States now intends to respond to China as soon as possible regarding the latest [missing word] on the point of contention regarding consular jurisdiction.

Polish Government Represses the Communist Party 37

Declares the Party's Existence Illegal

Warsaw, 15th (Reuters dispatch) – Poland has announced that the existence of the Communist Party is illegal. This order was issued by the Minister of the Interior after the sentencing of the socialist party members who rioted in Warsaw last September.

Sudden Death of Japanese Privy Councilor Matsumuro 38

Tokyo, 16th (Dentsu dispatch) – Privy Councilor Matsumuro suddenly died of apoplexy today at 1 p.m. He had attended the Privy Council's careful examination committee on the election law amendment bill. After the meeting at 4 p.m., while discussing matters with government officials, he suddenly suffered a stroke and died. He was 81 years old. He served twice as Minister of Justice during the Katsura Cabinet and the Terauchi Cabinet. After resigning from his post, he served as a member of the House of Peers and is currently a Privy Councilor.

Central Committee and National Government Memorial Week 40

Central Party Headquarters: At 9 a.m. on February 16th, the Central Party Headquarters held the 99th weekly memorial service for the late Premier Sun Yat-sen in the main auditorium. Attending were Central Committee members Hu Hanmin, Chu Minyi, Ma Chaojun, Chen [missing name]ying, Wang Bailing, Yu Jingtang, officials from various departments and committees, and approximately 500 guests. Hu Hanmin presided over the meeting. After the ceremony, the chairman reported, stating briefly: "Since the Fourth Plenary Session decided on three training programs regarding the promotion of party affairs, the work of party members, and the rectification of party discipline, there is a clear direction. This should be regarded by all comrades as a motto to be followed without fail. It must be understood that serving the party requires consistent action, with no retreat, taking the requirements of the principles as a basis, and jointly striving for the demands of the entire political situation, thus meeting the hopes of the entire populace. The reason why there is a need to correct the current party affairs work is that there is a psychological error, believing that the warlords have been eliminated, the overall situation is gradually becoming unified, and the work of the party can be somewhat relaxed, without being very tense, and that reaching stability is sufficient, thinking that inaction is better than action. Therefore, the spirit of struggle and advancement is gradually decreasing. It is not known that in the destruction period, the revolutionary spirit was used to remove all obstacles, and now that it is the construction period, the responsibility is even more important and there are many obstacles. The work is turning negative, and how can this be explained? If the qin and se are not in tune, the strings can be changed and retuned. If, because of the lack of tune, the strings are discarded and not played, it is like choking oneself by refusing to eat, which is impossible. The party must combine doctrine and action as the axis of politics. If it loses its ability to act, then any cause must fall behind, so how can there be advancement, and how can there be construction? The Communist Party often uses insidious methods to divide the party. If we can unite as a whole, and the work of the doctrine is increasingly tense, then their plans will not be successful, and the elimination of the Communist disaster will not be difficult. The spirit of the party is in knowledge, benevolence and courage, and the application of knowledge and benevolence depends on courage to achieve it. Willingness to sacrifice is great courage. Looking at past history, whether military, political or party affairs, if the person in charge has the determination to sacrifice, there is no reason for failure. Now, the ambition of the reactionaries and imperialists has not been completely abandoned, and the actions of the party must not be relaxed. Even when the reactionaries are eliminated and the imperialists hand over power, there must be actions to adapt to the needs to prepare for unforeseen events, and we must not be careless and waste our efforts. Although there is no single path to training, the main point is to keep acting and be willing to sacrifice. For all matters concerning the people, which are things that the party ought to do, mobilize at any time without retreating. Furthermore, we must act in unison with a spirit of unity, gather the strength of the masses, and make a great mobilization of the whole. The two words training are related and connected, like governing an army. If there is training without practice, then male energy will decrease, and it will be difficult to improve work efficiency." After the report, the meeting adjourned at 10 a.m.

National Government: At 10 a.m. on the same morning, the National Government held the weekly memorial service for the late Premier Sun Yat-sen. Attending were Chiang Kai-shek, Hu Hanmin, Wang Chonghui, Zhu Peide, Wang Boqun, Chu Minyi, Liu Yufen, Liu Shangqing, Ma Fuxiang, Wei Daoming, Lin Xiang, Liu Ruiheng, Niu Shuijian, He Yaozu, Zhang Huichang, Li Shuhua, Zheng Hongnian, Chen Yi, Zhang Wohua, Chen Shaokuan, Zhou Yawei, and over two hundred officials from the National Government's civil service and military affairs departments. Chiang Kai-shek presided over the meeting. Hu Hanmin gave a speech, stating briefly: "The two sentences in the party song, 'loyally diligent, bravely courageous, faithfully trusting,' are instructions given by the late Premier Sun Yat-sen to the students of the military academy. The meaning is not only addressed to the military academy, because revolutionaries should have the determination to sacrifice and the courage to self-examine in order to restore the spirit of the nation. Recently, officials often commit the evils of laxity, negligence, complacency, and seeking ease. The National Government has followed the resolutions of the Fourth Plenary Session and issued instructions to reform politics, which people should follow. Now that the Control Yuan has been established and the candidates for the Control Committee have been announced, it is hoped that all working comrades will have the spirit of observing the law and acting in the public interest, practicing loyalty, diligence, trust, and banishing the bad habits of lethargy and lack of energy. If they still cannot fulfill their duties, they will not be forgiven by the people. As for the powers of the Control Yuan as stipulated in the National Government Organization Law, there are two points: impeachment and audit. The purpose of the censorate system of the Qing Dynasty was only to correct the monarch's mistakes, and its greatest responsibility was limited to speaking out. The current situation is very different. Apart from reactionaries, everyone inside and outside the party has the right to speak. If there are errors in policies, they should be corrected by the party headquarters, which is not within the scope of the Control Yuan's powers. The candidates for the Control Committee who have now been announced all have considerable histories. It is hoped that they will appropriately impeach the powers they are responsible for, and not be too ambitious and hasty, or be too lax and aim to establish a truly honest government."

Zhang Xueliang's Talk with a Group of Japanese Reporters 41

Shenyang Correspondence: Zhang Xueliang, the Deputy Commander, at the request of Shibayama, the Japanese advisor to the Border Defense Headquarters, received a group of Japanese reporters at the Border Defense Headquarters at 4 p.m. on the 10th. He gave a talk on the current situation, with the following main points: (1) On the issue of the Northeast's relationship with the Central Government, Zhang said that as a member of the Central Government, he naturally supports the Central Government. The Party Affairs Guidance Committee has been established here, but when it will formally begin its work is still under study. His personal opinions on the Kuomintang have been proposed at the Fourth Plenary Session and are on record, and he will naturally remain consistent. (2) On the issue of military expenditures for the Northwest Army and the Shanxi Army, he said that the expenses of the Shanxi Army are borne by Shanxi Province, while the expenses of the Northwest Army are borne by the Central Government. The expenses of the Central Army are paid by the Central Government, and the expenses of the local armies are borne by the local governments. (3) On the issue of the organization of the Deputy Commander's Headquarters, he said that the headquarters of the Deputy Commanders of the Army, Navy, and Air Force will definitely be established in Beiping. Since he became the Deputy Commander, his political duties have become increasingly heavy, and he wants to transfer the position of Commander of the Border Defense to someone more capable, but it is not convenient to force anyone to take over, so for now, he has to hold the position himself. (4) On the issue of the replacement and transfer of the chairmen of the Northeast provinces, he said that there are many rumors about this matter, but the appointment, removal, and transfer of the chairmen of the provinces cannot be decided solely by him. Therefore, the talk of transferring the chairmen is not likely to materialize at this time. (5) On the issue of suppressing the Communist Party, he said that among the Communist Party, there is a distinction between those who study doctrines and those who plan riots. He has ordered the police and other agencies to strictly suppress the rioters. However, this issue is also related to the security of Japan, and he is willing to work with Japan to thoroughly suppress them. (6) On the issue of abolishing likin and subsequent arrangements, he said that the abolition of likin is indeed something that the Central Government should do, and the Central Government should subsidize the impact on the local finances. However, local governments must also reduce government expenses to alleviate the burden on the people. (7) On the issue of negotiations with Japan on railways, he said that there is currently no need to negotiate with Japan on the current state of railway transportation in the Northeast. Kimura, the director of the South Manchuria Railway Company, has been dispatched to Shenyang, probably to take the opportunity to conduct research on business matters. As for the rumors about the railway network plan proposed by the Northeast Transportation Committee, they are purely fabricated rumors and have no basis, so there is no need to explain them.

The Northern Financial Conference Concludes 42

No Results on Various Budget Proposals

Twenty-Two Proposals Have Been Announced

Zhang Zhao, Chairman of Chahar and Hebei Provinces, Comes to Shenyang

Shenyang Correspondence: The Northern Financial Conference, which opened on January 26th, concluded on February 10th. Excluding the two days of recess in the middle due to Sundays, there were thirteen plenary sessions. Due to the large discrepancies between income and expenditure in the budget proposals of the provinces and cities, no results were achieved. Other matters relating to currency and surtaxes resulted in 76 proposals, of which 22 have been announced. There is no definite date for the announcement of the rest. As for the various budget proposals that have not yet been decided, they will be submitted to the Political Committee for discussion and decision. At the meeting on the 11th, Zhang Xueliang summoned all members to his private residence. Zhang also telegraphed Liu Yifei, Chairman of Chahar Province, and Wang Shuchang, Chairman of Hebei Province, to come to Shenyang to join the discussion on the budget proposals. Liu has replied that he will come to Shenyang on the 15th to spend the New Year. Wang has not yet replied because he is inspecting troops in Tianjin. (12th)

The Three Eastern Provinces Establish an Office for Purchasing and Transporting Local Products 43

Shenyang Correspondence: The economy of the Northeast is declining and becoming increasingly precarious, a phenomenon rarely seen before. The authorities believe that this is due to the fall in prices of local products. It has been found that the export of local products from the Northeast has always been in the hands of foreign merchants. Since the recent gold-silver price changes and other factors, many foreign merchants have been hesitant to move forward. The Northern Financial Conference decided to have the governments of the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang jointly raise large sums of money and jointly organize a special product purchase and transportation office to purchase large quantities of local products for direct export and sale to the interior, in order to raise the prices of local products, break the deadlock, and change the environment. The transport and sales methods are divided into three phases. A special product purchase and transport office will be established in the official banks of the three eastern provinces and will begin operations immediately. The articles of association are as follows: (1) The provincial governments of the three eastern provinces will organize a special product purchase and transport office for the purchase and transport of special products. (2) The office will have one director, four deputy directors, and a number of clerks. (3) The head office will be located in the official bank of the three eastern provinces, and branch offices will be established in suitable locations as needed. (4) The personnel of the head office and branch offices will be concurrently staffed by personnel from various banks and businesses and will not receive additional salaries. Other expenses will be paid from official expenses. (5) The director will be responsible for all affairs of the entire office, and the deputy directors will assist him. (6) Each branch office will have one director, and the number of clerks will be determined by the complexity of the affairs. (7) The special product office will specialize in the purchase and transport of grains and beans, the special products of the three provinces, for export at any time. Purchases will be made in phases. The first phase will purchase 30,000 cars, the second phase 20,000 cars, and the third phase 10,000 cars. (8) After the establishment of the special product office, it will open for business on February 11th. (9) The detailed rules for the special product office will be determined separately. (10) These articles of association will be implemented after the establishment of the office. (11) These articles of association may be amended at any time if there are any matters that have not been fully addressed. (11th)

Tragic Fire at the Fushun Coal Mine 44

Rumors of 3,000 Chinese Workers Killed or Injured

The Japanese Side Claims No One Was Injured

Shenyang Correspondence: The Liaoning National Diplomacy Association has learned that a fire suddenly broke out at 11:50 a.m. on the 8th in the Dayama Main Pit No. 18 of the Fushun South Manchuria Railway Coal Mine. The Japanese side immediately sealed off the mine entrance. There are rumors that 3,000 Chinese workers were killed. The association immediately dispatched Che Xiangchen, the director-general of the Common Sense Promotion Association, and members Hao Keyong and Li Zhengwen, to investigate the matter to determine the truth. Che returned on the 11th. According to him, after arriving in Fushun, he first went to the Education Bureau and the Library to inquire, but he could not find any clues. He then disguised himself and went to the vicinity of the coal mine to investigate, and talked with the miners to find out, but he could not find out the details, and he was interfered with and prevented by the Japanese police and guards. Finally, he met with a certain reporter who was familiar with the situation of the Japanese side and asked about this matter. According to him, a fire did break out in the mine pit, due to a miner mistakenly handling sulfur on a rock. About 2,000 to 3,000 Chinese workers were killed or injured. However, according to the Japanese side's subsequent propaganda, the day was a Sunday and the miners were resting, so no one was injured. However, there are the following doubts: (1) Even on Sundays, there are workers in the mine pit. The Japanese side's propaganda that no one was injured is an overcorrection. (2) When the fire broke out, many family members of the miners went to the side of the pit to see what was happening. Reports said that up to 3,000 people died, but the Japanese side later claimed that no one was injured. The contradiction is too great. Che also said that this accident was due to poor equipment. We should find ways to investigate the actual number of deaths and injuries so that we can negotiate with the Japanese side on the basis of reason and ask them to compensate for the losses.

Another report states that a large fire broke out in the West Second Strip of the Dayama Main Pit of the South Manchuria Railway Coal Mine on the night of the 7th, and many Chinese workers died, a very tragic situation. It is common for Chinese workers to die unnaturally in coal pits due to fires and floods. The current report is about a more severe disaster. The reporter had a lot of trouble finding out the truth. Later, I met a friend who I have known for a long time and who is now employed in a coal mine. Only then did I learn a little about the situation when the fire broke out. The reason was that the equipment in the pit was not good and the temperature was too high, which caused the sulfur in the coal to burn, and the fire was very fierce. In order to protect the coal mine, the mine authorities immediately sealed the entrance, so most of the Chinese workers who were working at the time (reportedly more than 3,070 people) and a small number of Japanese staff (about 30 to 40 people) were killed. The tragic scene of the workers suddenly encountering this disaster, struggling and screaming, is unbearable to imagine. However, the Japanese side is still denying it.

After Ye Yixiong is Transferred to Shenyang, the Local Court Holds a Public Trial 45

Ye Admits to Jealousy, But Not to Plotting for Wealth

Reasons for the High Court's Ruling to Transfer the Case to Shenyang

Shenyang Correspondence: The case of Ye Yixiong, the former trial judge of the Special District Local Court, for the murder of Zhang Liqing, has been transferred to Shenyang by the judicial authorities of Liaoning Province on the order of Commander Zhang. Ye was transferred to Shenyang on the 8th. However, Zhang Liqing is still being treated in Harbin due to her injuries and has not yet arrived in Shenyang. After Ye was transferred to Shenyang, the Local Court sent him to the prison for detention, and the prosecutor Xue [missing character]ping conducted several investigations. The public prosecution was filed on the 10th. At 10 a.m. on the 11th, the Local Court specially opened a trial in the criminal court. The president of the court, Tang Yinfen, presided. Prosecutor Xue [missing character]ping also appeared in court. At 10:20, Ye was brought out of the prison. Ye wore a blue woolen overcoat and a Turkish fur hat. His appearance was haggard. First, the judge briefly interrogated him. Then, the prosecutor stood up to present the indictment, saying that Ye Yixiong's murder of Zhang Liqing was filed by the Special District Court Prosecutor's Office on charges of encroachment and murder, which was not inappropriate. [missing character] the original indictment and requested the court to make a public judgment according to law. [missing character] the judge interrogated Ye about the murder. Ye confessed without hesitation. [missing character] only confessed that he committed the crime because of jealousy and did not admit that he plotted to kill for wealth. Finally, the judge stood up and announced that the case would be adjourned until the plaintiff arrived in court and a new date was set for the trial. [missing character] then the court adjourned, [missing character] still sent to the prison by the bailiffs for detention.

The Criminal Court ruled that Ye Yixiong's premeditated attempted murder and encroachment case was to be transferred to the Shenyang Local Court of Liaoning Province by the Criminal Court of the Northeast Branch of the Supreme Court, based on the application of the prosecutor of the Northeast Branch of the Supreme Court. [missing character] The reasons for the ruling are as follows: The applicant stated that the defendant Ye Yixiong, who previously served as a candidate trial judge of the Eastern Province Special Region Local Court, was prosecuted by the Binjiang Local Court for premeditated attempted murder and encroachment. Now, the Northeast Political Affairs Committee has telegraphed that the Binjiang Court's trial judge in the Ye Yixiong case is suspected of being unfair, and the office should apply to the Northeast Branch of the Supreme Court for a ruling to designate the Shenyang Local Court as the first [missing character] court and report it for handling. In response to this, the court found that the court where Ye Yixiong originally served and the Binjiang Local Court were in the same region. Although the personnel of the Binjiang Local Court are not necessarily all connected with the defendant, the trial is still likely to be biased. Therefore, in accordance with Articles 21 and 22 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the application should be transferred to the Shenyang Local Court of Liaoning Province for jurisdiction to show judicial authority. According to Article 21 of the Criminal Procedure Law, if a court suspects that a trial may be unfair due to special circumstances, the higher court may transfer the case to another court of the same level within its jurisdiction as the original court. In this case, the defendant's premeditated murder and encroachment case has been referred to the Binjiang Local Court for the first [missing character] trial. It was found that the defendant was originally a candidate trial judge of the Eastern Province Special Region Local Court, and the Binjiang Local Court is in the same region, so it is difficult to guarantee that the trial will be unfair. The application of the applicant should be considered reasonable. In accordance with Article 23 of the Criminal Procedure Law, it should be ruled that this case should be transferred to the Shenyang Local Court of Liaoning Province for first instance jurisdiction.

After the Shanxi Military Division Commanders Take Office 46

Each Army Will Be Downsized After the Demobilization Funds Arrive

Shang Zhen Remains Calm Recently

Taiyuan Correspondence: The issue of downsizing the Shanxi Army has now been resolved. The newly appointed military division commanders have also telegraphed their assumption of office. However, the issue of the road protection army and the garrison is still a major stumbling block to the future of downsizing. The proposed plan was agreed upon by the military commanders and Ji, Hu, Shang, Xu, etc. after several discussions. In addition to Ji and Hu reporting to Shenyang, Ji, Hu, Shang, and Xu jointly telegraphed Zhang for instructions, and advocated that the military commanders should telegraph their assumption of office first. At that time, the military commanders were deeply afraid that after telegraphing their assumption of office, all issues would be said to be subject to compliance, and there would be no way to say anything. Therefore, they advocated telegraphing Zhang for instructions first and then deciding on the policy of assuming office after the reply telegram arrived. [missing character] Fang agreed, and the assumption of office telegram was issued on the 9th. The date at the end of the telegram was written as the character Yu. It is said that Zhang Xueliang sent a telegram on the 7th, ordering that the Tianjin resolution be followed and the organization be carried out quickly. After much research, it was agreed that since the implementation of demobilization required [missing character] to assume office, it was better to assume office before Zhang's telegram, which could show considerable [missing character] attitude. This is where the telegram came from. Zhang's telegram did not mention the road protection army, the garrison, the military committee, and other issues. As for the military commanders, [missing character] there were not many meetings on that day, and their attitude was not as active as in the previous few days. It is currently planned to proceed in separate defense areas after the 2 million yuan of demobilization funds raised by Zhang in Tianjin are remitted.

The local security issue, which is related to the demobilization issue, is now becoming increasingly serious. Robberies are rampant in various counties in southern and eastern Shanxi. Even in the provincial capital, two incidents have occurred in the past two or three days. Guo Su, the magistrate of Linjin County, was recently shot and killed by bandits. Currently, almost all street talk is based on this news. Shanxi, which has been a paradise for the past twenty years, will soon be transformed into a den of bandits.

Shang Zhen's attitude has been extremely calm recently. In addition to agreeing to relinquish the position of military commander at an appropriate time, he has recently stated that he will not take the position of director of civil affairs and will temporarily maintain the old director, Qiu Yangjun. Shang made a statement to reporters yesterday on the aftermath of the Shanxi situation, saying that after the military division commanders of the Shanxi-Suiyuan army sent out telegrams assuming office, it has come to an end. Although Zhang (Xueliang) has not received a reply to his request for a change in the approach to the generals, it has been approved. As for Sun Chu, the commander of the Fifth Division, who was listed in the telegram, he has been appointed as commander of the road protection army. The missing division commander has been appointed by Li Fuying. The generals plan to return to their respective defense areas within a few days to begin to handle the demobilization of their troops. Because the people of Shanxi bear 7 million yuan per month, while the total revenue of the province is only over 1 million yuan per month, the difference between income and expenditure is huge. Therefore, the people's request to cancel the one-yuan surcharge cannot be resolved unless the provincial banknotes are somehow improved. I (Shang himself) am doing my best to urge the central government to implement the previously decided plan to reorganize the 24 million yuan of financial public bonds in Shanxi. Once these public bonds are issued, the Shanxi banknotes will definitely not be as sluggish as they are now, and the one-yuan surcharge will be canceled. As for the people's request to convert the arsenals into production facilities, I strongly agree, but a concrete plan must be drawn up before it can be implemented. As for the date of appointment of the provincial government committees, it has not yet been determined. (12th)

Important News Two

Lu Diping Resigns from His Positions as Chairman of Jiangxi Province and Commander-in-Chief 47

But the Central Government Still Tries to Persuade Him to Stay

Nanchang Correspondence: When Lu Diping succeeded Zhu Peide as Chairman of Jiangxi Province two years ago, he believed that the 12th, 18th, 50th divisions could eliminate the bandits and communists without any problems. Therefore, in his declaration of office, he expected to govern Jiangxi within three months and achieve results. However, after the campaigns against Tang Shengzhi and Zhang Fakui, and the Northern Expedition, only one brigade of the 12th Division and two brigades of the 18th Division remained in Jiangxi. As a result, the Communist bandits became increasingly rampant. Almost all 81 counties were devastated, and the suffering was everywhere. There was not enough time to save the dying, so [missing character] political construction and autonomy could not be discussed. Lu had therefore telegraphed the Central Government last year to impeach himself and resign from the position of Chairman of Jiangxi Province. The National Government issued an order to persuade him to stay. When Ji'an was lost last year, Chairman Chiang came to Jiangxi to supervise the army. Lu again personally resigned to Chiang. At this time, Chiang said that Lu was responsible for the military affairs of suppressing bandits on the front line and could not change generals in the face of battle. Chiang greatly encouraged Lu. Lu then went to Ji'an again to command the military affairs. However, in the battles of Longgang and Dongshao last year, Lu's main forces, the 18th and 50th divisions, suffered heavy losses. Lu became even more heartbroken. He returned to the province from Ji'an on the 3rd of this month and went to Nanchang Hospital to recuperate. He never went to the provincial government. Later, the 77th Division found the head of Division Commander Zhang in the Ji'an River. Lu wept bitterly at the provincial funeral and felt completely disheartened. He immediately sent a handwritten note to the secretary's office and the accounting department to prepare for the handover. At the same time, he telegraphed Chairman Chiang, requesting permission to resign from the position of Chairman of Jiangxi Province and Commander-in-Chief of the Ninth Route Army, so that he could rest. His resignation was very firm. However, it is heard that the Central Government still intends to persuade him to stay. In recent days, important official documents from the provincial government and the headquarters of the Ninth Route Army have still been sent to Nanchang Hospital for him to read. (12th)

I will never waste a penny, misuse a person, engage in corruption, or accept bribes. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment. This oath." After the oath supervisor gave a speech, Mr. Ge gave a reply. Local Correspondence

Songjiang 49

The Wang Family Near Tinglin Robbed: Brigand activities are rampant in the towns south of the Huangpu River, with incidents being recorded frequently. Only Tinglin Town has been somewhat peaceful since the army and police were stationed there for defense. Unexpectedly, at the Wang family's home, a former oil mill owner less than three miles south of the town, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived on the night of the 11th while they were just beginning to enjoy their dreams. They ransacked the place and looted all the clothes and silver dollars from each room, causing great unease among those nearby with some wealth.

Reporting of Total Number of Citizens in One District: The district offices of this county previously received orders to conduct citizen registration in order to prepare for future elections of local self-government personnel. It is now learned that the registration process has been completed. The number of men with citizen qualifications is 13,089, and the number of women is 2,444, totaling 15,533.

Suzhou 50

Child Bride Killed by Tobacco Pipe Head: Chen Yizhi, a Suqian native who makes a living pulling carts behind the Xinjianmen Road Wangshudun, took in Shi Tinghui's daughter, Shuigen, also from the same hometown, as a child bride for his eldest son, Gengsheng. This has been five years. Recently, he purchased peanuts and other items to prepare for the customary ancestral worship. Shuigen secretly ate some, so he immediately used the head of a dry tobacco pipe to strike Shuigen's left temple. She died the next day. Because the deceased's parents are both deceased, her uncle, Shi Biao (resident at No. 12 Huaiyang Road, Malu), filed a complaint with the local court. On the 15th, an investigating officer was dispatched to examine the wound, and it was also discovered that the deceased had multiple burn marks on her body, proving that she had been abused before her death. Therefore, Chen was immediately taken into custody to await interrogation and investigation.

Wuxi 51

Tragic Capsizing: Bodies Retrieved: It is reported that the Hengyi small steamer, belonging to the Litai Steamer Company of this county, suddenly capsized and sank to the bottom of the river in front of the Zhenyuan Silk Factory at the South Gate on the 14th, causing the drowning deaths of many passengers. It is now learned that after receiving the report yesterday, the county court's procuratorate immediately dispatched Assistant Prosecutor Zhu Zonghai, along with examiners, to the scene of the incident for a thorough inspection. Since the hull was submerged, nothing could be seen. The director of the Third Public Security Sub-bureau, Wang Weixin, led bureau members Qin Rui and police officers to meet with Prosecutor Zhu. They hired a Tongli Steamer from the Maoxin Flour Mill in the West Gate and borrowed hoisting equipment from the factory, also employing over a dozen laborers to assist. It was not until 7 p.m. that the sunken steamer was lifted out of the water. A total of seven male bodies were found in the cabin: Mi Hefang, accountant of the Wuxi Newspaper Office; Yang Quanbao of Xinchangxiang Hardware Store; Wang Yongxi from Anzhen; Xu (Xu is currently an employee of the 11th Sub-bureau); Qian Fufu; Gu Yonggen, the owner of the Jiu Yu Cosmetics Shop; and an unnamed old man. The female corpses of Zhu Sulin and Aunt Zou were also retrieved. Prosecutor Zhu ordered Shen to examine each of the male and female corpses according to the law. After the examination, wooden plaques were prepared with the names written on them for the relatives of the deceased to identify the bodies. Upon hearing the news, the relatives of the deceased rushed to identify the bodies, creating a scene of grief and lamentation that was unbearable to witness. It is also heard that there are still bodies in the river, but it may not be easy to retrieve them all at once.

Unauthorized Holiday for Lunar New Year: The County Party Rectification Committee previously learned that the private Wuxi Middle School in the county had fabricated excuses to grant an unauthorized holiday for the Lunar New Year. It specially requested the Provincial Party Rectification Committee to find a way to stop this. Yesterday, the committee issued an order from the Provincial Party Rectification Committee stating that, according to the previous report, requesting a referral to stop the private Wuxi Middle School in Wuxi County from fabricating excuses to grant unauthorized Lunar New Year holidays, etc., the Education Department had been notified to stop it. Now, a reply has been received, stating that the school's fabrication of excuses and unauthorized granting of Lunar New Year holidays violates regulations. In addition to ordering the Wuxi County Magistrate to strictly order the school to convene all students for classes immediately, it should be reported for punishment if it continues to disobey. A corresponding reply is hereby issued for reference. This order.

Yesterday (the 14th), County Magistrate Li ordered the Public Security Bureau to detain Wu Shanbao.

Changshu 53

Meningitis Claims Three Lives in One Family: An epidemic of meningitis has recently been discovered in the Datandang area of Yuanhe District, spreading extremely rapidly. The son of farmer Fan Junhua in the village suddenly contracted the disease and died despite efforts to save him. Less than two days later, his second son also contracted the disease and passed away. Unexpectedly, soon after the funeral arrangements were made, the youngest son also became ill and died in less than three hours. Within five days, the family lost three lives, which is truly tragic.

Zhenjiang 54

Business Community Discusses the Issue of Business Opening During the Abolished Lunar New Year: The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce believes that since merchants across the country have universally adopted the Gregorian calendar, all customs related to the abolished Lunar New Year should also be abolished. A joint meeting of various trade associations and representatives of shops was convened yesterday at 2 p.m. Since the number of attendees did not meet the legal quorum, it was changed to an informal discussion. The discussion resulted in the decision that, during the reorganization period of each shop, those who do not want to reorganize can operate as usual, but even those who need to reorganize their accounts and inventory should maintain the original state. A notice was sent to all businesses yesterday for general knowledge.

Heavy Snow in Zhenjiang: Since the beginning of winter, Zhenjiang has experienced a lot of rain and snow. In the past few days, there was first heavy rain, then hail, and then sudden heavy snowfall, lasting for two days and two nights, with the snow depth reaching more than one and a half feet, which is rare in recent decades. The Zhenjiang-Yangzhou long-distance buses and small steamers have all been suspended as a result.

Administrative Ruling on Reclamation Dispute at Yongji Island: The Zhenjiang County Government has concluded its trial of the Yongji Island reclamation dispute and has issued a formal ruling, which has been submitted to the Department of Civil Affairs for approval. The criminal aspects will be directly submitted to the court for trial. The main text of the ruling is recorded below: (1) The rent for each mu of reclaimed land on the island in the 20th year of the Republic shall be 1.2 yuan, to be paid in full before March 15 of this year. Otherwise, the land will be leased to others. (2) The security deposit shall be 2 yuan per mu, to be paid in full when the wheat matures this year. It will be refunded in full when the lease is terminated. (3) The area of land to be reclaimed shall be measured according to the standard measurement system promulgated by the Ministry. The county government shall send personnel to jointly measure and allocate the land, based on the population of the farmers and their ability to cultivate, but not exceeding 15 mu at most. (4) The Yi Du Bureau shall recover the previous rent arrears from Zhou Lou. (5) The Yi Du Bureau's constitution shall be abandoned and a new one shall be established. (6) The request for a deposit of 2.1 yuan is rejected. (7) Liu Zhiru and others' intimidation of the masses, resistance to rent, and coercion and insult of Tao Buzhou shall be transferred to the court for investigation and speedy arrest. It is heard that Liu and others have been transferred to the court for detention.

Investigation of Accusations Against Two County Magistrates: Citizens Wu Boyang and others of Songjiang recently submitted a report to the Provincial Government accusing the county magistrate of that county, Jin, of violating the law and harming the people, dereliction of duty and harming the public, requesting his dismissal and punishment or transfer to the court for investigation and handling. In addition, citizens Ma Shuren and others of Kunshan, on the grounds that the county magistrate of that county, Hong Cai, protected his subordinates and officials, submitted a report to the Provincial Government requesting a thorough investigation. After receiving the report, the Provincial Government stated that if the accusations were true, it would be inappropriate. It has ordered the Department of Civil Affairs to investigate, verify, and report the matter.

Nantong 55

Communist Leader Arrested: The Nantong County Government, upon receiving a confidential telegram from the Provincial Government, ordered the Liu Haisha District Office to arrest Wang Xingxiang, the Executive Committee Member of the Party Branch in that district, on the 14th and send him to the Provincial Military Law Joint Trial Office for interrogation. The suspect Wang is the commander-in-chief of the 13th Route of the Communist Red Guards and also the leader of cadres in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River.

Stopping the Celebration of the Abolished Lunar New Year: The Party and government organs in Tongyi are implementing measures to stop the public from celebrating the abolished Lunar New Year. Police officers have been dispatched to tear down spring couplets pasted on the doors of houses, and all businesses have been ordered to open as usual on the 17th and 18th. All temples and monasteries will be closed for half a month, and the lighting of firecrackers and the beating of drums and gongs for flower lanterns are strictly prohibited. The various organs will be inspected by the County Rectification Committee.

Rugao 56

Murder Suspect Arrested and Sent to the County: At 2 p.m. today (the 11th), a farmer named Ma Lao'er from the Lu Port District brought in a carpenter named Wang and reported to the Third Precinct Office that his younger brother, Ma Xiwei'er, was lured out and murdered by Wang's two brothers on the fourth day of the sixth lunar month this year (according to the lunar calendar). The incident was immediately reported, and local police and militias searched for the suspect, but the suspect had been evading capture for several months. Unexpectedly, the suspect was encountered yesterday afternoon in the Wan Hong Pawnshop. The report stated that an interrogation was immediately conducted, but the suspect Wang stubbornly denied the accusations. Officer Meng immediately sent Wang the carpenter and the witness to the county bureau for transfer to the county government for interrogation.

Gaoyou 57

Large-Scale Salary Demands by Teachers and Staff in Urban and Rural Areas: The education sector in this county is currently owed salaries for five months. Previously, the directors of various social education organizations and the principals of various schools went to the county government to discuss the matter with County Magistrate Wang, who agreed to first pay one and a half months' salary. However, yesterday (the 13th), heavy snow suddenly fell, preventing the funds collected from the grain transport depots in the four rural areas from being delivered to the city. Therefore, the previously agreed-upon payment of one and a half months' salary was difficult to implement. Upon receiving this news, teachers and staff in urban and rural areas gathered at the Education Bureau at 4 p.m. yesterday to ask Director Sun to go to the county government to request County Magistrate Wang to maintain his promise. They continued until 1 a.m. this morning without any results and dispersed. This afternoon at 3 p.m., teachers and staff in urban and rural areas will still go to the Education Bureau to sit and demand their salaries.

Xiaoshan 58

Major Cloth Store Goes Bankrupt: The cloth store, a well-known establishment in the Xiaoshan urban area, was once the leading cloth store in Xiaoshan. However, in recent years, the owner has been withdrawing large sums of money, and the manager, Zhu Jiaxian, passed away last winter, resulting in a lack of management. After inventory, it was found that there was a deficit of over 10,000 yuan. After offsetting the inventory, it was still insufficient to cover the expenses. It has been agreed that the store will close after a major clearance sale on February 15th, and a separate inventory will be conducted.

Number of Flood Victims Along the River in Yingsheng Township: In Yingsheng Township along the river in Xiaoshan, villagers were affected by the floods last winter, with a total of over 3,950 mu of farmland being flooded. There are a total of 124 affected households, with 249 adult males and females and 248 children, resulting in losses of 20,000 gold yuan. The township office and preparatory office have prepared a disaster map and submitted it to the Fifth District Office, requesting the county government to quickly provide emergency relief to help the victims.

Eight Poor People in the Riverside Area Frozen and Starved to Death: In the Dongsha Riverside Township of Xiaoshan, the sand land of the local sand people has been repeatedly eroded by the river, resulting in the loss of all crops. During this time of great cold, the poor people have no clothes or food and are sitting and waiting to die, which is a very miserable situation. In the past few days, five people have been frozen to death and three have starved to death. District Chief Yu Bin of the Sixth District has telegraphed the provincial and county governments, requesting assistance.

The Xu Brothers Can Be Called Brothers in Trouble: Xu Naiguang, the village chief of Wutu Village in Taoyuan, Xiaoshan, was previously reported by the public for collecting excessive land reporting fees of 0.2 yuan per mu. After investigation by the provincial and county governments, the accusations were confirmed, and he was fined 200 yuan. At the same time, Xu Naicao, Xu Naiguang's brother, who is the magistrate of Suian County in Shandong Province, embezzled public funds of over 2,500 yuan. The Shandong Provincial Government has sent a letter to the Zhejiang Provincial Government, ordering the Xiaoshan County Government to seal up his residence for compensation. The two brothers, one fined and the other having his property sealed, can be called brothers in trouble.

Merchants Robbed in Broad Daylight: Unbelievable: On the 13th, merchants collecting debts in the Keqiao area of Shaoxing were robbed on the road in Dongyun Qianqing Town. Because the road was muddy due to the heavy snow, they were stopped by five bandits who looked like soldiers. One bandit choked the merchant, while the other three robbed him of over 60 yuan in cash and a gold ring he was wearing. There were many passersby, but the area was close to the official road and there were few pedestrians, so they had to let them rob.

Hefei 59

Yishengxiang Robbed on Shizijie: At 8:30 p.m. on the 9th, during a snowstorm, five bandits suddenly appeared at Yishengxiang Cloth Store, the most prosperous area of Shizijie North. Two bandits stood guard outside, while three bandits went inside, raised their pistols to threaten silence, and went straight into the shop, broke open the cash counter, and searched for over 160 silver dollars and over 20 paper dollars. Not satisfied, they broke open the clothing boxes of the shop assistants and searched them thoroughly before fleeing.

Letters to the Editor

Letter from Former Yangzhong County Magistrate Xu Zusheng 60

The news about Yangzhong County's political affairs published in your newspaper these days is not factual. I would like to briefly state the following: (1) Zusheng resigned due to overwork and repeatedly pleaded before being approved. Zusheng has been in charge of Yangzhong for two years and has a very good relationship with the people of Yangzhong. There was no matter of waiting at the wharf and not allowing him to leave. (2) Construction funds were collected and remitted immediately during Zusheng's tenure, and there was never any misappropriation. However, the collection of various outstanding amounts from the former Finance Bureau's collection staff has been ordered to be expedited, but has not yet been cleared. The successor can continue to handle it, and Zusheng has no responsibility to repay it. The Construction Department has not consulted the Civil Affairs Department to investigate the matter. (3) The Yangzhong Baojin Island rent has always been collected by the county government. Recently, it was ordered to be transferred to the Zhenjiang Education Bureau for collection, and it has been complied with. Although the transfer procedures are complicated, they have not yet been completed. The successor can continue to handle it, and the Education Department has not withheld or ordered him to stay in Yangzhong for handover. (4) On the 3rd of last month, the Second District Office reported the discovery of a female corpse. I immediately went to inspect it and interrogated the suspects in the county that night. The case file is accurate and not difficult to investigate. There was no matter of taking the opportunity to escape. In short, this time Zusheng's resignation and handover of Yangzhong County Magistrate has been approved, and all handover procedures have been done clearly and without any mistakes. I hereby request that you check and make corrections. Xu Zusheng. February 13th.

The curriculum standards for teacher training courses in senior high schools have been compiled and printed. Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued an order to the education bureaus of various provinces and cities to forward them to various normal schools and senior high school teacher training courses for trial and research. The order stated that the provisional standards for various curricula, including kindergarten, elementary school, junior high school, senior high school general courses, and senior high school business courses, which were formulated by the Ministry, have been promulgated successively. Now, the provisional standards for teacher training courses in senior high schools have been printed and, in addition to distributing them, two copies are enclosed. The bureau is requested to ascertain the number of public and private senior high school teacher training courses and normal schools under its jurisdiction, and purchase the standards directly from the bookstores selling them. Forward them to the respective schools for practical trials, and forward the results of the trials and research to the Ministry for review. This order.

He Jian Cables Request for Independent Education Funding in Hunan Province 62

Regarding the case of independent education funding in Hunan Province, the Education Department of the province previously recommended representatives to come to Beijing to petition for it. Yesterday, the Chairman of the Provincial Government, He Jian, sent a cable to the Executive Yuan for the sake of education funding. The original telegram stated that Hunan Province's education funding relies solely on the salt tax surcharge of a small amount per bag of ocean salt, which is planned by the Finance Department. The Education Department has repeatedly submitted petitions and sent representatives to Beijing to petition for the implementation of a surcharge of 1.5 yuan per bag, approved by the Executive Yuan, to complete education independence and to allocate funds. The Finance Department is complying with the order to abolish the levy and has no ability to supplement education funding. Education is the foundation of construction, and funding is the lifeblood of education. It is feared that the future of education in Hunan Province will be considered and the approval of the surcharge will be completed to promote education, etc.

National Student Anti-Drug Essay Contest 65

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association has been holding a national student anti-drug essay contest for years to promote anti-drug education. There have been many excellent works. This year is the third year, and the Association has completed its preparations. It will send a circular to the principals of all large and medium-sized schools across the country. It has now prepared over 1,700 copies and will mail them to various provinces in the near future, along with the guidelines and registration forms. The topics are as follows:

(A) "University Group" (1) Discuss the malpractices of opium monopoly from a legal standpoint; (2) Study the tragic consequences of opium monopoly from an economic perspective; (3) Discuss the harm of opium monopoly from the perspective of national health; (4) The opium monopoly policy that is intolerable from a humanitarian point of view; (5) Opium monopoly is sufficient to create a total bankruptcy of social morality; (6) The Party's discipline does not allow the existence of opium monopoly; (7) Opium monopoly will inevitably violate the international anti-smoking treaties of previous sessions; (8) Predict the inevitable failure of opium monopoly from the history of smoking ban; (9) Opium monopoly is an obstacle to the implementation of political training; (10) The conspiracy of the great powers to implement the opium monopoly on small and weak nations. Choose one topic from the above. (B) "Middle School Group" Opium monopoly violates the President's anti-drug teachings. It is heard that the university group plans to take five to ten places, and the middle school group plans to take thirty to fifty places. In addition to medals and certificates, the first place will be awarded 100 yuan in cash. Registration details will be mailed immediately upon request from the Shanghai Association.
